03166: 
03167:   RequestOptions _setStreamType<T>(RequestOptions requestOptions) {
03168:     if (T != dynamic &&
03169:         !(requestOptions.responseType == ResponseType.bytes ||
03170:             requestOptions.responseType == ResponseType.stream)) {
03171:       if (T == String) {
03172:         requestOptions.responseType = ResponseType.plain;
03173:       } else {
03174:         requestOptions.responseType = ResponseType.json;
03175:       }
03176:     }
03177:     return requestOptions;
03178:   }
03179: 
03180:   String _combineBaseUrls(String dioBaseUrl, String? baseUrl) {
03181:     if (baseUrl == null || baseUrl.trim().isEmpty) {
03182:       return dioBaseUrl;
03183:     }
03184: 
03185:     final url = Uri.parse(baseUrl);
03186: 
03187:     if (url.isAbsolute) {
03188:       return url.toString();
03189:     }
03190: 
03191:     return Uri.parse(dioBaseUrl).resolveUri(url).toString();
03192:   }
03193: }

00160:             Globals().lopDaoTaoModel.value = classResp.first;
00161:           }
00162:         } catch (e) {
00163:           logError("refreshStudentInfo fetch class error: $e");
00164:         }
00165:

00167:         try {

00171:             responseUser.idBacDaoTao,

00174:             Globals().nienKhoaDaoTaoModel.value = cohortResp.first;
00175:           }
00176:         } catch (e) {
00177:           logError("refreshStudentInfo fetch cohort error: $e");
00178:         }
00179:       }

00001: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
00002: import 'package:get/get.dart';
00003: import 'package:vnu_core/common/log.dart';
00004: import 'package:vnu_core/common/utils.dart';

00008: import 'package:vnu_core/vnu_core.dart';
00009: 
00010: class VcoreProfilePassController extends GetxController {
00011:   BuildContext? context;
00012: 
00013:   RxBool isLoading = false.obs;
00014:   RxList<LoaiMatKhauModel> listLoaiMatKhau = RxList([]);
00015:   Rxn<LoaiMatKhauModel> loaiMatKhau = Rxn();
00016: 
00017:   // Doi mat khau
00018:   String oldPassword = '';
00019:   String newPassword = '';
00020:   String reNewPassword = '';
00021: 
00022:   @override
00023:   void onInit() {
00024:     super.onInit();
00025:     fetchPasswordType();
00026:   }
00027: 
00028:   fetchPasswordType() async {
00029:     //
00030:     try {
00031:       var response = await ApiRepository().getDanhSachLoaiMatKhau();
00032: 
00033:       listLoaiMatKhau.value = response;
00034:       for (var item in listLoaiMatKhau) {
00035:         if (item.key == 'Default') {
00036:           loaiMatKhau.value = item;
00037:         }
00038:       }
00039:       if (listLoaiMatKhau.isNotEmpty && loaiMatKhau.value == null) {
00040:         loaiMatKhau.value = listLoaiMatKhau.first;
00041:       }
00042:     } catch (e) {
00043:       snackBarError(e.toString());
00044:     }
00045:   }
00046: 
00047:   quenMatKhau() async {
00048:     if (loaiMatKhau.value == null) {
00049:       snackBarWarning('Bạn cần chọn loại hình nhận mật khẩu');
00050:       return;
00051:     }
00052:     try {
00053:       Utils.showProgress(context);
00054:       var reponse =
00055:           await ApiRepository().putQuenMatKhau(loaiMatKhau.value?.key ?? '');
00056:       Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00057:       Get.back(closeOverlays: true);
00058:       snackBarSuccess(
00059:           'Mật khẩu mới đã được gửi qua ${loaiMatKhau.value?.label} cho bạn.');
00060:     } catch (e) {
00061:       Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00062:       snackBarError(e.toString());
00063:     }
00064:   }
00065: 
00066:   thayDoiMatKhau() async {
00067:     if (loaiMatKhau.value == null) {
00068:       snackBarWarning('Bạn cần chọn loại hình nhận mật khẩu');
00069:       return;
00070:     }
00071:     if (oldPassword.isEmpty || newPassword.isEmpty || reNewPassword.isEmpty) {
00072:       snackBarWarning(
00073:           'Các trường thông tin không được để trống và chứa khoảng trắng.');
00074:       return;
00075:     }
00076:     if (newPassword != reNewPassword) {
00077:       snackBarWarning('Mật khẩu mới không trùng nhau.');
00078:       return;
00079:     }
00080:     //
00081:     logWarning(oldPassword);
00082:     logWarning(newPassword);
00083:     logWarning(reNewPassword);
00084:     //
00085: 
00086:     try {
00087:       Utils.showProgress(context);
00088:       var reponse = await ApiRepository().putCapNhatMatKhau(
00089:           loaiMatKhau.value?.key ?? '', oldPassword, newPassword);
00090:       Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00091:       snackBarSuccess(
00092:           'Mật khẩu của bạn đã được thay đổi thành công. Vui lòng đăng nhập lại.');
00093:       Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 2), () {
00094:         Globals().clearSession();
00095:         VnuCore().gotoLogin();
00096:       });
00097:     } catch (e) {
00098:       Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00099:       snackBarError(e.toString());
00100:     }
00101:   }
00102: }

00027:       var response = await ApiRepository().getAllAnhCanNhan();
00028: 
00029:       listAnhCaNhan.value = response;
00030:     } catch (e) {
00031:       snackBarError(e.toString());
00032:     }
00033:   }
00034: 
00035:   pickPhoto() async {
00036:     //

00038:     final XFile? image = await picker.pickImage(source: ImageSource.gallery);
00039: 
00040:     if (image != null) {
00041:       logSuccess('Pick file success...');

00043:       Utils.showProgress(context);
00044:       try {
00045:         var response = await ApiRepository().uploadAnhCanNhan(
00046:           File(image.path),
00047:         );
00048: 
00049:         listAnhCaNhan.add(response);
00050:         Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00051:       } catch (e) {
00052:         Utils.dismissProgress(context);
00053:         snackBarError(e.toString());
00054:       }
00055:     } else {
00056:       // User canceled the picker
00057:       logError('Pick file error...');
00058:     }
00059:   }
00060: 
00061:   deleteAnhCaNhan(AnhCaNhanModel image) async {
00062:     if ((image.guid ?? '').isEmpty) {
00063:       return;
00064:     }
00065:     try {
00066:       var _ = await ApiRepository().deleteAnhCanNhan(image.guid ?? '');
00067:       listAnhCaNhan.remove(image);
00068:     } catch (e) {
00069:       snackBarError(e.toString());
00070:     }
00071:   }
00072: }

00091:   void _sortServices(List<BoxServiceModel> services) {
00092:     List<String> priority = ["XemThoiKhoaBieu", "DiemMonHoc", "TheSinhVien"];
00093:     services.sort((a, b) {
00094:       int aIndex = priority.indexOf(a.loaiBoxDichVuEnum ?? '');
00095:       int bIndex = priority.indexOf(b.loaiBoxDichVuEnum ?? '');
00096:       if (aIndex == -1 && bIndex == -1) return 0;
00097:       if (aIndex == -1) return 1;
00098:       if (bIndex == -1) return -1;
00099:       return aIndex.compareTo(bIndex);
00100:     });
00101:   }
00102: 
00103:   void _loadCacheService() {
00104:     VnuCacheFileManager().getCacheFile(_kCacheKeyListDichVu).then((data) {
00105:       try {
00106:         var dataString = data ?? '';
00107:         if (dataString.isEmpty) return;
00108:         var dataJson = jsonDecode(dataString) as List;
00109:         List<BoxServiceModel> listObj = [];
00110:         for (var element in dataJson) {
00111:           try {
00112:             BoxServiceModel? model;
00113:             if (element is Map<String, dynamic>) {
00114:               model = BoxServiceModel.fromJson(element);
00115:             } else if (element is Map<dynamic, dynamic>) {
00116:               model = BoxServiceModel.fromJson(element.toStringDynamic());
00117:             }
00118:             if (model != null) {
00119:               if (model.loaiBoxDichVuEnum?.mapTypeBoxService() !=
00120:                   HomeService.XemLichThi) {
00121:                 listObj.add(model);
00122:               }
00123:             }
00124:           } catch (e) {
00125:             logError(e.toString());
00126:           }
00127:         }
00128:         _sortServices(listObj);
00129:         if (_services.isEmpty && mounted) {
00130:           setState(() {
00131:             _services = listObj;
00132:             _isLoading = false;
00133:           });
00134:         }
00135:       } catch (e) {
00136:         logError(e.toString());
00137:       }
00138:     });
00139:   }
00140: 
00141:   Future<void> _loadService() async {
00142:     try {
00143:       var response = await ApiRepository().getBoxServices();
00144:       response = response
00145:           .where(
00146:             (element) =>
00147:                 element.loaiBoxDichVuEnum?.mapTypeBoxService() !=
00148:                 HomeService.XemLichThi,
00149:           )
00150:           .toList();
00151:       _sortServices(response);
00152:       if (mounted) {
00153:         setState(() {
00154:           _services = response;
00155:           _isLoading = false;
00156:         });
00157:       }
00158:     } catch (e) {
00159:       if (mounted) setState(() => _isLoading = false);
00160:       logError(e.toString());
00161:     }
00162:   }

00538:   void _handleNaviService(HomeService? service) {

00544:         Get.to(() => const VcoreCamNangView());
00545:         break;
00546:       case HomeService.DangKyNoiTru:
00547:         Get.to(() => const DRMyRegistrationScreen());
00548:         break;
00549:       case HomeService.DiemMonHoc:
00550:         Get.to(() => const VcoreCoursePointsView());
00551:         break;
00552:       case HomeService.HuongDanSuDung:
00553:         Get.to(() => const VcoreHdsdView());
00554:         break;
00555:       case HomeService.MucHoiDap:
00556:         Get.to(() => const VcoreQuestionView());
00557:         break;
00558:       case HomeService.ThuTucMotCua:
00559:         Get.to(() => const VcoreOneDoorView());
00560:         break;
00561:       case HomeService.TimPhongTro:
00562:         Get.to(() => const VcoreMotelView());
00563:         break;
00564:       case HomeService.XemLichThi:
00565:         Get.to(() => const VcoreExamScheduleView());
00566:         break;
00567:       case HomeService.XemThoiKhoaBieu:
00568:         Get.to(() => const VcoreExamScheduleView());
00569:         break;
00570:       case HomeService.PhanAnhHienTruong:
00571:         Get.to(() => const VcorePahtView());
00572:         break;
00573:       case HomeService.DongBo:
00574:         Get.to(() => const VcoreSyncView());
00575:         break;
00576:       default:
00577:         break;
00578:     }
00579:   }

00047:   Future<SigninResponse> signin(
00048:       String username, String password, String deviceToken) async {
00049:     final response = await _dio.post<Map<String, dynamic>>(
00050:       '/api/auth/signin',
00051:       data: {
00052:         'username': username,
00053:         'password': password,
00054:         if (deviceToken.isNotEmpty) 'deviceToken': deviceToken,
00055:       },
00056:       options: Options(
00057:         headers: {
00058:           'Accept': 'application/json',
00059:           'Content-Type': 'application/json',
00060:         },
00061:       ),
00062:     );
00063: 
00064:     final result = SigninResponse.fromJson(response.data ?? {});
00065:     if ((result.accessToken ?? '').isEmpty) {
00066:       logError('Signin response does not contain access token: ${response.data}');
00067:     }
00068:     return result;
00069:   }

00099:       final String json = await _apiClient.getListTopics();
00100:       final Iterable l = jsonDecode(json);
00101:       return l.map((e) => e.toString()).toList();
00102:     } catch (e) {
00103:       logError(e.toString());
00104:       return [];
00105:     }
00106:   }
00107:

00109:     int pageIndex,

00115: 
00116:   Future<List<BoxServiceModel>> getBoxServices() async {
00117:     try {
00118:       final String json = await _apiClient.getBoxServices();
00119:       final Iterable l = jsonDecode(json);
00120:       final List<BoxServiceModel> services = List<BoxServiceModel>.from(
00121:           l.map((model) => BoxServiceModel.fromJson(model)));
00122:       services.sort((a, b) => a.thuTu.compareTo(b.thuTu));
00123:       return services;
00124:     } catch (e) {
00125:       return HomeService.values
00126:           .map((e) => BoxServiceModel(loaiBoxDichVuEnum: e.ordinal))
00127:           .toList();
00128:     }
00129:   }

00100:   Future<void> _checkBio() async {
